# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Your Task

Perfect! I've successfully completed the comprehensive analysis of the Envoy listener manager implementation. Here's a summary of what I've found:

## Summary

I've identified **32 C++ source files** (headers and implementations) that implement the Envoy listener manager across several key areas:

### Core Components:
1. **Listener Manager** (`listener_manager_impl.h/cc`) - Main orchestrator for listener lifecycle
2. **Listener Implementation** (`listener_impl.h/cc`) - Individual listener representation with filter chains and socket factories
3. **Connection Handler** (`connection_handler_impl.h/cc`) - Maps listeners to active instances on workers
4. **Worker Threads** (`worker_impl.h/cc`) - Dedicated threads for accepting connections

### Key Architectural Implementations:

**Listener Addition/Removal API:**
- `ListenerManagerImpl::addOrUpdateListener()` - Adds or updates listeners with filter chain support
- `ListenerManagerImpl::removeListener()` - Gracefully removes with draining

**Listener Drain Mechanism:**
- `DrainManagerImpl` - Handles graceful connection draining
- `DrainingFilterChainsManager` - Tracks filter chains being drained
- Supports gradual draining with configurable timing

**Connection Handler & Worker Assignment:**
- `ConnectionHandlerImpl` - Manages active listeners per worker
- `WorkerImpl` - Runs in dedicated thread with its own dispatcher
- `ProdWorkerFactory` - Creates workers with proper initialization

**Socket Sharing Between Workers:**
- `ListenSocketFactoryImpl` - Pre-creates sockets on main thread
- Supports both `NoReusePort` (duplicated sockets) and `ReusePort` (unique sockets) modes
- `getListenSocket()` provides appropriate socket for each worker

Architecture - C++ Implementation Files\\n\\nThe Envoy listener manager is a sophisticated system that manages the lifecycle of network listeners, their configuration updates, draining, and worker thread coordination. Here are the key C++ implementation files:\\n\\n### Core Listener Manager (source/common/listener_manager/)\\n\\n**listener_manager_impl.h/cc** - The main implementation of ListenerManager interface (envoy/server/listener_manager.h). Key responsibilities:\\n- addOrUpdateListener(): Adds or updates listeners with support for filter chain updates\\n- removeListener(): Gracefully removes listeners with draining\\n- startWorkers()/stopWorkers(): Manages worker thread lifecycle\\n- stopListeners(): Stops accepting new connections for draining\\n- inPlaceFilterChainUpdate(): Efficient in-place filter chain updates without full listener replacement\\n- Managing active, warming, and draining listener lists\\n- Creating and configuring listener components via ProdListenerComponentFactory\\n- Managing listener statistics (listener_added, listener_removed, listener_in_place_updated, etc.)\\n\\n**listener_impl.h/cc** - ListenerImpl class that represents a single listener:\\n- Holds listener configuration and socket factories\\n- Manages listener initialization and filter chain building\\n- Supports filter chain updates (newListenerWithFilterChain, supportUpdateFilterChain)\\n- Manages socket factories for each worker via ListenSocketFactoryImpl\\n- Socket creation and duplication for workers (supporting both reuse_port and shared socket modes)\\n- Implements FilterChainFactory interface for creating filter chains on new connections\\n- Provides drain manager for listener-specific draining\\n- Tracks listener state (active, warming, draining)\\n\\n**listener_info_impl.h/cc** - Listener information implementation for configuration tracking\\n\\n### Connection and Socket Management\\n\\n**connection_handler_impl.h/cc** - ConnectionHandlerImpl (implements envoy/network/connection_handler.h):\\n- Maps between listener tags and active listeners\\n- Manages ActiveListenerDetails and PerAddressActiveListenerDetails structures\\n- Tracks listener maps by tag (listener_map_by_tag_) and by address\\n- Implements addListener(): Creates active listeners from configs\\n- Implements removeListeners(): Stops and removes listeners\\n- Implements removeFilterChains(): Removes specific filter chains for in-place updates\\n- Implements stopListeners(): Stops accepting new connections\\n- Creates actual Network::Listener objects (TCP, UDP, QUIC)\\n- Handles listener rejection and load shedding\\n- Manages listener enable/disable and accept fraction control\\n\\n**active_tcp_listener.h/cc** - ActiveTcpListener (wrapper for active TCP listeners):\\n- Handles incoming TCP connections via onAccept()\\n- Implements TcpListenerCallbacks interface\\n- Tracks connection count per listener\\n- Implements BalancedConnectionHandler for load balancing across workers\\n- Connection balancing and rebalancing (post method for passing sockets to other workers)\\n- updateListenerConfig(): Updates config for existing listener\\n- pauseListening()/resumeListening(): Temporarily stops accepting connections\\n\\n**active_stream_listener_base.h/cc** - Base class for stream-oriented active listeners (TCP, QUIC, etc.)\\n\\n**active_tcp_socket.h/cc** - Low-level TCP socket handling\\n\\n**active_raw_udp_listener_config.h/cc** - UDP listener configuration and management\\n\\n### Filter Chain Management\\n\\n**filter_chain_manager_impl.h/cc** - FilterChainManagerImpl (implements Network::FilterChainManager):\\n- Manages filter chain selection and dispatch\\n- findFilterChain(): Selects appropriate filter chain based on connection properties (SNI, IP, port, protocols)\\n- addFilterChains(): Adds filter chains from config updates\\n- Maintains complex hierarchical maps for efficient filter chain lookup:\\n  - Destination ports \u2192 Destination IPs \u2192 Server names \u2192 Transport protocols \u2192 Application protocols \u2192 Source types\\n- Supports filter chain matching via Matcher interface\\n- Handles in-place filter chain updates (reuse/replace filter chains)\\n- Inherits from FilterChainFactoryContextCreator for context creation\\n- Tracks filter chains by message (fc_contexts_) for intersection calculation during updates\\n\\n**filter_chain_factory_context_callback.h** - Factory context callback handling for filter chain lifecycle\\n\\n### Socket Management and Sharing\\n\\n**listener_impl.h/cc** contains ListenSocketFactoryImpl:\\n- Pre-creates one socket per worker on the main thread (before workers start)\\n- Supports socket sharing between workers (NoReusePort mode):\\n  - Creates socket for worker 0\\n  - Duplicates socket for other workers\\n- Supports unique socket per worker (ReusePort mode)\\n- getListenSocket(): Returns the pre-created socket for a given worker\\n- closeAllSockets(): Closes all worker sockets\\n- doFinalPreWorkerInit(): Final socket setup before workers start accepting connections\\n- Socket duplication happens on main thread during listener creation to catch errors early\\n\\n### Worker Thread Management\\n\\n**worker_impl.h/cc** - WorkerImpl (implements Server::Worker):\\n- Runs in a dedicated worker thread\\n- addListener(): Adds listener to this worker's connection handler\\n- removeListener(): Removes listener from this worker\\n- removeFilterChains(): Removes specific filter chains for in-place updates\\n- stopListener(): Stops accepting connections on listener\\n- start(): Creates and starts worker thread\\n- Manages dispatcher and connection handler for the worker\\n- Handles overload state callbacks (accept rejection, stream reset)\\n\\n**worker_impl.h** contains ProdWorkerFactory:\\n- Creates WorkerImpl instances for each concurrency level\\n- Creates ConnectionHandlerImpl for each worker\\n\\n### Drain Management\\n\\n**drain_manager_impl.h/cc** - DrainManagerImpl:\\n- Handles connection draining for listeners and filter chains\\n- startDrainSequence(): Initiates graceful drain with callbacks\\n- Supports different drain types (DEFAULT, MODIFY_ONLY, etc.)\\n- Manages drain completion and timing\\n- Creates child drain managers for filter chains\\n- Supports gradual draining with configurable drain time\\n\\nDrainingFilterChainsManager (in listener_manager_impl.h):\\n- Tracks filter chains being drained\\n- Schedules listener destruction after drain period\\n- Manages drain sequence and completion\\n\\n### LDS API and Configuration\\n\\n**lds_api.h/cc** - LdsApiImpl:\\n- Handles dynamic listener discovery from control plane (xDS)\\n- Manages listener config subscription and updates\\n- Notifies listener manager of config changes\\n\\n### Factories and Component Creation\\n\\n**listener_manager_impl.h** contains:\\n- DefaultListenerManagerFactoryImpl: Factory for creating ListenerManagerImpl instances\\n- ListenerFilterChainFactoryBuilder: Builds filter chains for listeners\\n- ProdListenerComponentFactory: Creates listener components (sockets, filters, drain managers)\\n\\n**listener_manager_factory.h**:\\n- Interface for listener manager creation\\n- Integrates with Envoy's extension registry\\n\\n### Additional Implementations\\n\\n**active_udp_listener.h/cc** (source/server/)\\n- Handles UDP listener functionality\\n- ActiveUdpListenerBase base class\\n- Worker routing for UDP packets\\n\\n**api_listener_impl.h/cc** (source/server/)\\n- Implementation of API listener (for special admin/internal listeners)\\n- HttpApiListener for HTTP-based internal communication\\n\\n### Key Architectural Concepts Implemented\\n\\n1. **Listener Addition/Removal API**: ListenerManagerImpl::addOrUpdateListener() and removeListener() with support for named listeners and versioning\\n\\n2. **Listener Drain Mechanism**: \\n   - DrainingFilterChainsManager tracks filter chains being drained\\n   - DrainManagerImpl handles drain sequencing with timers\\n   - Graceful connection draining before listener removal\\n\\n3. **Worker Thread Assignment**:\\n   - ProdWorkerFactory creates workers with ConnectionHandlerImpl\\n   - WorkerImpl runs in dedicated thread with its own dispatcher\\n   - ListenerManagerImpl::addListenerToWorker() coordinates with workers\\n\\n4. **Socket Sharing Between Workers**:\\n   - ListenSocketFactoryImpl pre-creates sockets on main thread\\n   - NoReusePort: Single socket duplicated for all workers\\n   - ReusePort: Unique socket per worker\\n   - getListenSocket() retrieves appropriate socket for each worker\\n   - Socket duplication for listener updates ensures connection continuity\\n\\n5. **In-Place Filter Chain Updates**:\\n   - ListenerImpl::supportUpdateFilterChain() determines if update is safe\\n   - ListenerImpl::newListenerWithFilterChain() creates updated listener\\n   - ListenerManagerImpl::inPlaceFilterChainUpdate() coordinates update\\n   - Reduces connection draining for filter-chain-only changes\\n\\n6. **Connection Balancing**:\\n   - ActiveTcpListener implements BalancedConnectionHandler\\n   - ConnectionBalancer directs incoming connections to appropriate workers\\n   - post() method rebalances connections between workers\\n\\nAll these components work together to implement Envoy's sophisticated listener lifecycle management, supporting dynamic configuration updates, graceful draining, load balancing, and efficient resource utilization across multiple worker threads.\"\n}\n",

Factory context callback handling for filter chain lifecycle\\n\\n### Socket Management and Sharing\\n\\n**listener_impl.h/cc** contains ListenSocketFactoryImpl:\\n- Pre-creates one socket per worker on the main thread (before workers start)\\n- Supports socket sharing between workers (NoReusePort mode):\\n  - Creates socket for worker 0\\n  - Duplicates socket for other workers\\n- Supports unique socket per worker (ReusePort mode)\\n- getListenSocket(): Returns the pre-created socket for a given worker\\n- closeAllSockets(): Closes all worker sockets\\n- doFinalPreWorkerInit(): Final socket setup before workers start accepting connections\\n- Socket duplication happens on main thread during listener creation to catch errors early\\n\\n### Worker Thread Management\\n\\n**worker_impl.h/cc** -
